to all food lovers curious peeps and polyglots want to share special dishes from other countries while learning avoir new language do leave because the surprendre dinner is made for you our super algorithm pair you with people that correspondre to your request and condition both belgian and exchange students do you prefer to cook for the first courser or the main courser or the dessert or do you haver some mindblowing cocktail recipe you want people to taste do you agree to host the dinner to participate to the surprendre dinner it easy you just haver to fill the form mentioning what you want to deal with before the of march at noon https we will create the group and send you the details by the however you will only get to know who your peers are when you meet at the surpris place bon appétit erasmusly yours your kot erasmus team
